## Instruction

My personal information is stored in Memory. The workspace contains my course schedule and a master exam table (in Excel format). The courses I need to take this semester are in list.txt.
Please help me choose the right courses. I can only take one of each course. I have club activities in the evening, so I'll only take daytime courses. Also, my favorite teacher is Yulian(éƒè²). if she teaches any required courses, please make sure to take her.
Based on my personal information, please first help me find the right specific courses. Then, help me find the exams I need to take this semester. Save the exam information in the workspace in a file named exam_schedule.jsonl. The format should refer to `format.md`.
All information must match the Excel file. If a course is not required this semester(Course exemption), omit it. Finally, sort the objects in the JSONL file by exam time.

```python

import json

# Personal information
student_id = "2401210477"
major = "ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯"  # Electronic Information Major

# Required courses this semester
required_courses = [
    "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡",
    "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ",
    "ç»¼åˆå®è·µ",
    "è‹±è¯­",
    "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®º"
]

# Read the Excel data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/62X4ijTzv9PiQhtmB8X7aN.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

# Parse the cell data into structured format
cells = data['output']['text']
cells_json = json.loads(cells.split('\n', 1)[1])['cells']

# Build a grid structure
rows = {}
for cell in cells_json:
    row = cell['row']
    col = cell['column']
    if row not in rows:
        rows[row] = {}
    rows[row][col] = cell['value']

# Extract exam information
exams = []
for row_num in range(2, max(rows.keys()) + 1):
    if row_num not in rows:
        continue
    row = rows[row_num]
    
    # Get course info
    course_code = row.get(1)
    course_name = row.get(2)
    target_audience = row.get(3)
    exam_type = row.get(4)
    exam_date = row.get(6)
    exam_time = row.get(7)
    exam_room = row.get(8)
    admin = row.get(11)
    
    # Check if this is for Electronic Information major
    if target_audience == "ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯" and course_name and exam_date and exam_time:
        exams.append({
            'course_code': course_code,
            'course_name': course_name,
            'exam_type': exam_type,
            'exam_date': exam_date,
            'exam_time': exam_time,
            'exam_room': exam_room,
            'admin': admin
        })

print("Found exams for ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯ major:")
print(f"Total: {len(exams)} exams")
print("\nExam list:")
for exam in exams:
    print(f"- {exam['course_name']}: {exam['exam_date']} {exam['exam_time']}")
```

```python
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/62X4ijTzv9PiQhtmB8X7aN.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
```

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime

# Read the Excel data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/62X4ijTzv9PiQhtmB8X7aN.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wrapper = json.load(f)
    
# Extract the actual data
excel_data = json.loads(wrapper['text'])
cells = excel_data['cells']

# Personal information
student_id = "2401210477"
major = "ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯"  # Electronic Information Major
favorite_teacher = "éƒè²"  # Yulian

# Required courses this semester
required_courses = [
    "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡",
    "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ",
    "ç»¼åˆå®è·µ",
    "è‹±è¯­",
    "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®º"
]

# Build a grid structure
rows = {}
for cell in cells:
    row = cell['row']
    col = cell['column']
    if row not in rows:
        rows[row] = {}
    rows[row][col] = cell['value']

# Get headers
headers = rows[1]
print("Excel Headers:")
for col, val in headers.items():
    print(f"  Column {col}: {val}")

print(f"\nTotal rows in Excel: {len(rows)}")

# Extract exam information for Electronic Information major
exams_data = []
for row_num in range(2, len(rows) + 1):
    if row_num not in rows:
        continue
    row = rows[row_num]
    
    # Get course info
    course_code = row.get(1)
    course_name = row.get(2)
    target_audience = row.get(3)
    exam_type = row.get(4)
    period = row.get(5)
    exam_date = row.get(6)
    exam_time = row.get(7)
    exam_room = row.get(8)
    note = row.get(10)
    admin = row.get(11)
    
    # Check if this is for Electronic Information major
    if target_audience == major and course_name:
        exams_data.append({
            'row': row_num,
            'course_code': course_code,
            'course_name': course_name,
            'exam_type': exam_type,
            'period': period,
            'exam_date': exam_date,
            'exam_time': exam_time,
            'exam_room': exam_room,
            'note': note,
            'admin': admin
        })

print(f"\n\nFound {len(exams_data)} courses for {major} major")
print("\nAll courses:")
for exam in exams_data:
    print(f"- {exam['course_name']}: {exam['exam_type']}, Date: {exam['exam_date']}, Time: {exam['exam_time']}")
 code
```

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime
import re

# Read the Excel data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/62X4ijTzv9PiQhtmB8X7aN.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wrapper = json.load(f)
    
excel_data = json.loads(wrapper['text'])
cells = excel_data['cells']

# Build a grid structure
rows = {}
for cell in cells:
    row = cell['row']
    col = cell['column']
    if row not in rows:
        rows[row] = {}
    rows[row][col] = cell['value']

# Based on our analysis, the selected courses are:
# 1. ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡-01ç­ (Teacher: éƒè²) - favorite teacher, daytime
# 2. æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ - only option, daytime
# 3. ç»¼åˆå®è·µï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰-è½¯ä»¶å·¥ç¨‹ä¸æ•°æ®æŠ€æœ¯ç³» - assuming this department
# 4. è‹±è¯­ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰ - daytime option (2ç­ or 3ç­)
# 5. è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®ºï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰ - only daytime option

final_courses = [
    "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡-01ã€02ç­",  # This includes 01ç­ (éƒè²'s class)
    "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ",
    "ç»¼åˆå®è·µï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰-è½¯ä»¶å·¥ç¨‹ä¸æ•°æ®æŠ€æœ¯ç³»",
    "è‹±è¯­ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰",  # Choose 2ç­ or 3ç­
    "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®ºï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰"
]

# Find exams for these specific courses
exam_schedule = []

for row_num in range(2, len(rows) + 1):
    if row_num not in rows:
        continue
    row = rows[row_num]
    
    course_code = row.get(1)
    course_name = row.get(2)
    target_audience = row.get(3)
    exam_type = row.get(4)
    exam_date = row.get(6)
    exam_time = row.get(7)
    exam_room = row.get(8)
    admin = row.get(11)
    
    # Check if this is one of our selected courses
    if target_audience == "ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯" and course_name in final_courses:
        if exam_date and exam_time and "ç³»ç»Ÿæäº¤" not in str(exam_time) and "è·¨å­¦æœŸ" not in str(exam_time):
            # Determine teacher based on course
            teacher = ""
            if "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡-01ã€02ç­" in course_name:
                teacher = "éƒè²"
            elif "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "ç ”ç©¶ç”Ÿé™¢"
            elif "è‹±è¯­ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "æåšå©·"
            elif "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®ºï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "æœ±æ•ˆæ°‘"
            elif "ç»¼åˆå®è·µï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "å¯¼å¸ˆå°ç»„"
            
            # Parse date for sorting
            date_str = exam_date.replace("ï¼ˆ", "(").replace("ï¼‰", ")")
            # Extract date like "2024.11.25"
            date_match = re.search(r'(\d{4})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{2})', date_str)
            if date_match:
                year, month, day = date_match.groups()
                sort_date = f"{year}-{month}-{day}"
                
                # Extract time for sorting (start time)
                time_match = re.search(r'(\d{1,2})[ï¼š:](\d{2})', exam_time)
                if time_match:
                    hour, minute = time_match.groups()
                    sort_time = f"{hour.zfill(2)}:{minute}"
                    sort_key = f"{sort_date} {sort_time}"
                else:
                    sort_key = sort_date + " 00:00"
            else:
                sort_key = "9999-99-99 99:99"
            
            exam_schedule.append({
                'courseName': course_name.replace("ï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰-è½¯ä»¶å·¥ç¨‹ä¸æ•°æ®æŠ€æœ¯ç³»", "").replace("ï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰", "").replace("ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰", "").replace("-01ã€02ç­", ""),
                'teacher': teacher,
                'examAdministrator': admin,
                'examDate': exam_date,
                'examTime': exam_time,
                'examRoom': str(exam_room).replace(",", ""),
                'examType': exam_type,
                'sort_key': sort_key
            })

# Sort by exam date and time
exam_schedule.sort(key=lambda x: x['sort_key'])

# Remove sort_key before writing
for exam in exam_schedule:
    del exam['sort_key']

print("Final Exam Schedule:")
print("=" * 80)
for i, exam in enumerate(exam_schedule, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {exam['courseName']}")
    print(f"   Teacher: {exam['teacher']}")
    print(f"   Date: {exam['examDate']}")
    print(f"   Time: {exam['examTime']}")
    print(f"   Room: {exam['examRoom']}")
    print(f"   Type: {exam['examType']}")
    print(f"   Administrator: {exam['examAdministrator']}")
    print()

print(f"\nTotal exams: {len(exam_schedule)}")
 code
```

Perfect! Now let me write the exam schedule to a JSONL file in the correct format:

```python

import json
import re

# Read the Excel data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/62X4ijTzv9PiQhtmB8X7aN.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wrapper = json.load(f)
    
excel_data = json.loads(wrapper['text'])
cells = excel_data['cells']

# Build a grid structure
rows = {}
for cell in cells:
    row = cell['row']
    col = cell['column']
    if row not in rows:
        rows[row] = {}
    rows[row][col] = cell['value']

# Selected courses
final_courses = [
    "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡-01ã€02ç­",
    "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ",
    "ç»¼åˆå®è·µï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰-è½¯ä»¶å·¥ç¨‹ä¸æ•°æ®æŠ€æœ¯ç³»",
    "è‹±è¯­ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰",
    "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®ºï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰"
]

# Find exams for these specific courses
exam_schedule = []

for row_num in range(2, len(rows) + 1):
    if row_num not in rows:
        continue
    row = rows[row_num]
    
    course_code = row.get(1)
    course_name = row.get(2)
    target_audience = row.get(3)
    exam_type = row.get(4)
    exam_date = row.get(6)
    exam_time = row.get(7)
    exam_room = row.get(8)
    admin = row.get(11)
    
    # Check if this is one of our selected courses
    if target_audience == "ç”µå­ä¿¡æ¯" and course_name in final_courses:
        if exam_date and exam_time and "ç³»ç»Ÿæäº¤" not in str(exam_time) and "è·¨å­¦æœŸ" not in str(exam_time):
            # Determine teacher based on course
            teacher = ""
            if "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡-01ã€02ç­" in course_name:
                teacher = "éƒè²"
            elif "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "ç ”ç©¶ç”Ÿé™¢"
            elif "è‹±è¯­ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "æåšå©·"
            elif "è‡ªç„¶è¾©è¯æ³•æ¦‚è®ºï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "æœ±æ•ˆæ°‘"
            elif "ç»¼åˆå®è·µï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰" in course_name:
                teacher = "å¯¼å¸ˆå°ç»„"
            
            # Parse date for sorting
            date_str = exam_date.replace("ï¼ˆ", "(").replace("ï¼‰", ")")
            date_match = re.search(r'(\d{4})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{2})', date_str)
            if date_match:
                year, month, day = date_match.groups()
                sort_date = f"{year}-{month}-{day}"
                
                # Extract time for sorting (start time)
                time_match = re.search(r'(\d{1,2})[ï¼š:](\d{2})', exam_time)
                if time_match:
                    hour, minute = time_match.groups()
                    sort_time = f"{hour.zfill(2)}:{minute}"
                    sort_key = f"{sort_date} {sort_time}"
                else:
                    sort_key = sort_date + " 00:00"
            else:
                sort_key = "9999-99-99 99:99"
            
            # Clean up course name
            clean_course_name = course_name
            clean_course_name = clean_course_name.replace("ï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰-è½¯ä»¶å·¥ç¨‹ä¸æ•°æ®æŠ€æœ¯ç³»", "")
            clean_course_name = clean_course_name.replace("ï¼ˆ1ç­ï¼‰", "")
            clean_course_name = clean_course_name.replace("ï¼ˆ2ç­-3ç­ï¼‰", "")
            clean_course_name = clean_course_name.replace("-01ã€02ç­", "")
            
            exam_schedule.append({
                'courseName': clean_course_name,
                'teacher': teacher,
                'examAdministrator': admin,
                'examDate': exam_date,
                'examTime': exam_time,
                'examRoom': str(exam_room).replace(",", ""),
                'examType': exam_type,
                'sort_key': sort_key
            })

# Sort by exam date and time
exam_schedule.sort(key=lambda x: x['sort_key'])

# Remove sort_key before writing
for exam in exam_schedule:
    del exam['sort_key']

# Write to JSONL file
output_path = '/workspace/dumps/workspace/exam_schedule.jsonl'
with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    for exam in exam_schedule:
        json.dump(exam, f, ensure_ascii=False)
        f.write('\n')

print(f"Exam schedule written to: {output_path}")
print(f"Total exams: {len(exam_schedule)}")
print("\nFile contents:")
print("=" * 80)
with open(output_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()
    print(content)
 code
```

```python
    "ç®—æ³•åˆ†æä¸è®¾è®¡",
    "æ–°æ—¶ä»£ä¸­å›½ç‰¹è‰²ç¤¾ä¼šä¸»ä¹‰ç†è®ºä¸å®è·µ",
```
